    var EMBEDDED_CONSENT_COOKIE = 'embedded-consent';

    function writeCookie(name, value, duration) {
      var expires = new Date();
      expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + duration * (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
      document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; path=/; expires='+expires.toUTCString()+'; samesite=None; secure';
    }

    /* Sync the OneTrust consent to a SameSite=None cookie for use on embedded pages */
    function updateCookieForEmbeds(consented) {
      if (consented) {
          writeCookie(EMBEDDED_CONSENT_COOKIE, new Date().toUTCString(), 365);
      } else {
          writeCookie(EMBEDDED_CONSENT_COOKIE, new Date().toUTCString(), -1);
      }
    }

    var acceptBtn = document.getElementById('onetrust-accept-btn-handler'),
      recommendedBtn = document.getElementById('accept-recommended-btn-handler');

        updateCookieForEmbeds(true);
      });
    }
    if (recommendedBtn) {
      recommendedBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
        updateCookieForEmbeds(true);
      });
